dropping connections. It consists of several key components:\\n\\n**Core Architecture:**\\nThe mechanism is built on the HotRestart interface (envoy/server/hot_restart.h) which defines the contract for hot restart operations. HotRestartImpl (source/server/hot_restart_impl.cc) is the main implementation that coordinates between parent and child Envoy processes during restart.\\n\\n**Parent/Child Process Model:**\\nThe system uses a parent-child process architecture implemented through HotRestartingParent (source/server/hot_restarting_parent.cc) and HotRestartingChild (source/server/hot_restarting_child.cc), both extending HotRestartingBase (source/server/hot_restarting_base.cc). The base class provides shared RPC stream functionality (RpcStream class) for inter-process communication.\\n\\n**Socket Passing Mechanism:**\\nSocket file descriptors are passed between processes using Unix domain sockets with the SCM_RIGHTS control message type. The socket passing is coordinated through:\\n- RpcStream::sendHotRestartMessage() and receiveHotRestartMessage() in hot_restarting_base.cc which use CMSG (ancillary data) macros for sending/receiving file descriptors\\n- RpcStream::getPassedFdIfPresent() which extracts passed file descriptors using CMSG_FIRSTHDR, CMSG_DATA, and SCM_RIGHTS\\n- Listener socket duplication via HotRestartingChild::duplicateParentListenSocket() which retrieves listener sockets from the parent process\\n\\n**Message Protocol:**\\nCommunication between parent and child uses protobuf messages defined in source/server/hot_restart.proto with different request types:\\n- PassListenSocket: Request for listener socket file descriptor passing\\n- DrainListeners: Signal to start draining listeners\\n- Stats: Retrieve and merge parent statistics\\n- ShutdownAdmin: Shutdown parent's admin interface\\n- Terminate: Signal parent process termination\\n- ForwardedUdpPacket: Forward QUIC UDP packets between processes\\n\\n**Shared Memory:**\\nThe implementation uses POSIX shared memory (via HotRestartOsSysCalls interface in envoy/api/os_sys_calls_hot_restart.h) to maintain shared state like statistics and log locks. The attachSharedMemory() function in hot_restart_impl.cc manages the shared memory attachment during hot restart.\\n\\n**Drain Sequence:**\\nThe drain mechanism is implemented in DrainManagerImpl (source/server/drain_manager_impl.cc) which coordinates graceful shutdown of connections:\\n1. Parent receives drainParentListeners() signal from child\\n2. Parent starts DrainManagerImpl::startDrainSequence() to gracefully drain existing connections\\n3. Child registers ParentDrainedCallbackRegistrar callbacks (envoy/network/parent_drained_callback_registrar.h) to detect when parent has drained\\n4. UDP listeners use parent_drained_callback_registrar_ to delay listening until parent is fully drained\\n\\n**Listener Socket Reuse:**\\nThe ListenSocketImpl and UdpListenerImpl classes (source/common/network/listen_socket_impl.cc and source/common/network/udp_listener_impl.cc) integrate with the hot restart system by:\\n- Storing OptRef<ParentDrainedCallbackRegistrar> for UDP socket coordination\\n- Using listener_manager_impl.cc's duplicateParentListenSocket() calls to retrieve and reuse parent sockets\\n\\n**Child Readiness Signaling:**\\nChild process readiness is communicated through:\\n- HotRestartingChild::getParentStats() which requests parent stats\\n- HotRestartingChild::registerParentDrainedCallback() which registers callbacks for parent drain completion\\n- allDrainsImplicitlyComplete() signal when parent has been drained or terminated\\n- HotRestart::mergeParentStatsIfAny() which merges parent statistics into child\\n\\n**Integration Points:**\\nThe hot restart system is integrated into the main server flow through:\\n- source/server/server.cc which calls restarter_.drainParentListeners() during initialization\\n- source/exe/stripped_main_base.cc which creates HotRestartImpl during startup (configureHotRestarter)\\n- Server initialization calls HotRestart::initialize() after the event dispatcher is ready\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1556,"cache_read_input_tokens":93506,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1556},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e2907188-8010-496a-90b0-c2a010d95bc8","uuid":"4c6631e1-a93f-4e15-8b97-6164cc520391"}

dropping connections. It consists of several key components:\\n\\n**Core Architecture:**\\nThe mechanism is built on the HotRestart interface (envoy/server/hot_restart.h) which defines the contract for hot restart operations. HotRestartImpl (source/server/hot_restart_impl.cc) is the main implementation that coordinates between parent and child Envoy processes during restart.\\n\\n**Parent/Child Process Model:**\\nThe system uses a parent-child process architecture implemented through HotRestartingParent (source/server/hot_restarting_parent.cc) and HotRestartingChild (source/server/hot_restarting_child.cc), both extending HotRestartingBase (source/server/hot_restarting_base.cc). The base class provides shared RPC stream functionality (RpcStream class) for inter-process communication.\\n\\n**Socket Passing Mechanism:**\\nSocket file descriptors are passed between processes using Unix domain sockets with the SCM_RIGHTS control message type. The socket passing is coordinated through:\\n- RpcStream::sendHotRestartMessage() and receiveHotRestartMessage() in hot_restarting_base.cc which use CMSG (ancillary data) macros for sending/receiving file descriptors\\n- RpcStream::getPassedFdIfPresent() which extracts passed file descriptors using CMSG_FIRSTHDR, CMSG_DATA, and SCM_RIGHTS\\n- Listener socket duplication via HotRestartingChild::duplicateParentListenSocket() which retrieves listener sockets from the parent process\\n\\n**Message Protocol:**\\nCommunication between parent and child uses protobuf messages defined in source/server/hot_restart.proto with different request types:\\n- PassListenSocket: Request for listener socket file descriptor passing\\n- DrainListeners: Signal to start draining listeners\\n- Stats: Retrieve and merge parent statistics\\n- ShutdownAdmin: Shutdown parent's admin interface\\n- Terminate: Signal parent process termination\\n- ForwardedUdpPacket: Forward QUIC UDP packets between processes\\n\\n**Shared Memory:**\\nThe implementation uses POSIX shared memory (via HotRestartOsSysCalls interface in envoy/api/os_sys_calls_hot_restart.h) to maintain shared state like statistics and log locks. The attachSharedMemory() function in hot_restart_impl.cc manages the shared memory attachment during hot restart.\\n\\n**Drain Sequence:**\\nThe drain mechanism is implemented in DrainManagerImpl (source/server/drain_manager_impl.cc) which coordinates graceful shutdown of connections:\\n1. Parent receives drainParentListeners() signal from child\\n2. Parent starts DrainManagerImpl::startDrainSequence() to gracefully drain existing connections\\n3. Child registers ParentDrainedCallbackRegistrar callbacks (envoy/network/parent_drained_callback_registrar.h) to detect when parent has drained\\n4. UDP listeners use parent_drained_callback_registrar_ to delay listening until parent is fully drained\\n\\n**Listener Socket Reuse:**\\nThe ListenSocketImpl and UdpListenerImpl classes (source/common/network/listen_socket_impl.cc and source/common/network/udp_listener_impl.cc) integrate with the hot restart system by:\\n- Storing OptRef<ParentDrainedCallbackRegistrar> for UDP socket coordination\\n- Using listener_manager_impl.cc's duplicateParentListenSocket() calls to retrieve and reuse parent sockets\\n\\n**Child Readiness Signaling:**\\nChild process readiness is communicated through:\\n- HotRestartingChild::getParentStats() which requests parent stats\\n- HotRestartingChild::registerParentDrainedCallback() which registers callbacks for parent drain completion\\n- allDrainsImplicitlyComplete() signal when parent has been drained or terminated\\n- HotRestart::mergeParentStatsIfAny() which merges parent statistics into child\\n\\n**Integration Points:**\\nThe hot restart system is integrated into the main server flow through:\\n- source/server/server.cc which calls restarter_.drainParentListeners() during initialization\\n- source/exe/stripped_main_base.cc which creates HotRestartImpl during startup (configureHotRestarter)\\n- Server initialization calls HotRestart::initialize() after the event dispatcher is ready\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
